 Cuttack is the historic city of Odisha
 mana jaataa he ki 941 isvi main is nagar kii sthapana hui
 The city is located at the meeting point of the Mahanadi and its tributary, Kathjuri
 kareeb 9 sau saalon tak katak odisha kii rajdhani rahi
 Cuttack came under British occupation in 1803
 1826 main katak odisha kii rajdhani bani
 After independence, the capital of Odisha was shifted from Cuttack to Bhubaneswar in 1948
 ye vahi shahar he jahaan krantikari subhash chandra bose kaa janm hua tha
 Political Background Like other Lok Sabha seats in Odisha, the Congress, Janata Dal and Biju Janata Dal have dominated the Cuttack constituency
 1952 se lekar 1962 tak is seat par congress ne jeet hasil kii
 In 1967, Srinivas Mishra of Praja Socialist Party won the election
 1971 main congress ke janaki ballab patnayak chunaav jite
 In 1977, the Congress had to face defeat from this seat and Sharat Kumar Kar of the Janata Party emerged victorious
 1980 main congress ke tikat par janaki ballab patnayak ne phir vaapasi kii
 Shrikant Jena of Janata Dal won this seat in 1989
 jena ke jeet kaa safar 1991 main bhi jari rahaa
 With the formation of the Biju Janata Dal in December 1997, the politics of this parliamentary constituency also changed
 1998 main jab loksabhaa chunaav hue to bijedy ke bhartruhari mehataab chunaav jite
 After this, in the Lok Sabha elections of 99, 04, 09, 2014, Bhartrihari Mahatab continued to win on the BJD ticket
 saamaajik taana-banachunaav ayog ke aankadon ke mutabik 2014 loksabhaa chunaav ke dauraan katak loksabhaa kshetra main 13 lakh 71 hajaar 617 voters the
 There were 7 lakh 31 thousand 918 male voters, while the number of female voters was 6 lakh 39 thousand 699
 2014 loksabhaa chunaav main is seat par 71
 The turnout was 35 percent
 is loksabhaa seat par vidhansabha kii 7 siten hai
 These seats are Baramba, Banki, Atagarh, Barabati Cuttack, Chowdwar Cuttack, Cuttack Sadar, Khandapada
 2014 ke vidhansabha chunaav main in sabhi siton par biju janata dal ne jeet hasil kii thi
 2014 mandate Bhartrihari Mahtab received 5 lakh 26 thousand 85 votes in the 2014 Lok Sabha elections
 congress kii pratyaashee or abhinetri aparajita staradam ke baavjood bhi duusare number par raheen
 Aparajita got 2 lakh 19 thousand 323 votes

 hudahud naam oman ne diya he
 It is an Arabic word

 ab naam padane ke peeche kii vajah bhi jaan lijie
